Maybe it was the drugs, but deep down he knew that Kim Hyeyeon wasn't as strong as she believed everyone to be. Inside, she broke easily, and she had been broken for years, ever since it happened, he presumed. She walked around like that, put on a fake smile and smarted off to people like she was all put together, when in reality - there was barely anything left of her.

He knew everything she felt too well. All that she had went through she didn't deserve, it was a clear thing to understand, especially then. Since he'd seen it all go down himself, he knew Hyeyeon wasn't the one who really did that to Jisung all those years ago. It was all a cover up for their own doings, and it was wrong to have all been blamed on her.

His thoughts were cut short by the sound of her shaking voice. The way she spoke like she was a delicate feather, about to break from any contact, was enough to make him hold her in his arms tighter.

"I-I saw the one you shot, Haechan."
















***







The night sky was full of the bright stars, each and everyone peering down at the humans below. Alone, in the cold of such an October night, walked a boy dressed in his Halloween costume which he'd tried rather hard on. He was jingling the keys to his mother's Mustang with one hand, whilst the other was messing with his locks of caramel hair that wasn't covered by the hat, pulling at them in frustration.

Nothing could explain the anger Na Jaemin felt in his bones. He just couldn't seem to understand that if it hadn't been her ex boyfriend who spiked the drinks all the way in the kitchen of the school - who the hell had? He had been so sure no one would have gone back there, why would they really bother?

He couldn't come to the conclusion on if he really believed her ex or not. Sure, he'd known Jisung for a long time, but he was a completely different person now. Jaemin couldn't decipher if he was truly being honest or not.

So who did it?

The thought breaking question only continued to remain in his head as he walked through the parking lot. At that point, as his brown irises diverted to the moonlit sky above, he felt like those same stars beaming down where mocking him. For those stars had seen the culprit, hadn't they? He pleaded silently with them as he stared up above, as if he was expecting the sky to form a mouth and inform him.

He was stuck, completely lost in his own worries and debates. Whatever drug had been put in those drinks was a serious one, it seemed to be one he had never heard of before, not with those sort of side effects. Then again, it wasn't like he was informed in the drug world - but what kind of drug would cause you to have hallucinations like that? Hyeyeon had looked like she'd been thrown into a torture chamber, like someone had took her world and completely upturned it.

"fuck," he mumbles the profanity to himself. If it was the last thing he did, he was going to find out who did such a thing to her. Hyeyeon didn't deserve the shit that people constantly threw at her, not with how kind, sweet, and soft she tended to be under the hard shell which she hid under.

Perhaps there was another gang as DMHS he nor Jisung knew of. Maybe it was someone from the outside who snuck in, trying to play some sort of joke, or maybe it was someone unknown that was personally targeting her.

It didn't matter which one it was, he was going to find them.

The next worry that was floating in his cloud of thoughts was the fact she'd seemed to of disappeared. It wasn't smart of Jaemin to leave her by herself unknowingly of the effects the drug would have on her. He had just been so angered at Jisung, whom he believed full fledgedly had to be the culprit, that he couldn't help himself from wanting to make the boy his punching bag.

But he hadn't expected her to vanish when he came back. It worried the hell out of him, had someone helped her? If anything bad were to happen to her, how would ever manage to live with himself? It'd stay with him forever, he couldn't lose the one person in the entirety of his new school he liked.

The only thing he knew he could do was go to her house and pray that she was there. Surely, someone had just nicely brought her home, right?

He couldn't be so sure anymore. There were too many terrifying thoughts flying around in his head, so many that Jaemin was beginning to get a migraine. Everything was stressing him out, and he wanted nothing more than to see her, to know she was okay.

And find out who the hell put that in her drink.

Jisung's words back in the kitchen repeated in his head, sending chills up his spine in the form of needles. They pricked at his skin, created anxiety that swept through his veins. You know, we aren't the only gang in Chicago, it was something he had never stopped to think about.

But why? What would the motive be?

He didn't get it no matter how hard he tried to.

Groaning in frustration, Jaemin was just growing close to the mustang he had been driving recently. The white tint of the paint on the car seemed to call to him as he grew closer to it. His finger had just been hovering over the button to unlock the vehicle when something had pulled him out of his thoughts. It was a voice, one he hadn't expected to hear.

"Jaemin!" it was a scream coming from a direction he hadn't been sure of due to the shock he'd felt, "Jaemin, help!"

His head whips to every which side, confused as to what could possibly be happening. A part of him wished it was her, that he could find her and make sure she was okay. But then again, maybe she already was okay. Maybe she was safe back at home, sound asleep. He could only hope, assuming that best friend she talked so much of had saved her from the party.

It was when he saw it after the panic in his body had calmed down. Back in an alley way about ten feet away, in between the gym and the school, was Jisung's friend Jeno. He was the one who loved guns, and always carried one everywhere. Apparently he was a really great shot, but he had never seen him in action to know. And with the way he saw the boy on his knees, with a dark black figure standing above him, knife at his throat, he wasn't sure he ever would (not that he would want to.)

"Oh my god," were the only words he could think of as he tried to make out the face of the guy. If he had been at the party wearing a costume, he definitely wasn't anymore. He was wearing dark clothing so that he blended in with the dark night, a hood covering most of his face so his features weren't visible enough.

But one thing Jaemin could make out, as he made a bolt towards the two boys like a complete mad man, was the smirk that had spread across the killers lips as he effortlessly ran the knife across Jeno's throat. Jaemin's brown eyes bulged as he only forced himself to run faster, trying to catch whoever did it, to try to make anything out of what was happening right.

"Hey, come back!" he screamed as he had lost his breathe, being unable to keep up with the long strides of the killer, "I'll find whoever you are!"

But the culprit of such a dirty deed hadn't turned back to face him, or even get a mere glance of his face. In defeat and exasperation that what he just saw had really happened, the boy frantically turns back towards the body that was now lying on the concrete of the alleyway.

"Oh no, oh no," he chanted to himself as he ran up to Jeno's lifeless looking body. He'd been hoping that some sort of miracle would happen and the boy would still have any sort of pulse, but with the way the blood was creating a huge puddle around his body, there was no chance he was living.

He rises from having been crouched over, not wanting to get blood on his shoes or his costume. Jaemin runs a hand through his hair repeatedly, as if it would give him any sort of idea as to what he should do in this situation. Every time he looked back down to the body, the reality only sunk in his skin more and more. He just saw someone die, not only that, but it was someone he knew. He had only spoke to Jeno hours ago, right before he had left.

And although he was not fond of Jisung nor any of his friends that followed him around like fiends, that didn't mean he was heartless. The boy had been killed, and even though it most likely had to do with some sort of gang business he was better off not involved in, he still had to try to do the right think.

Pushing back his emotions, Jaemin hurriedly dials the boys number. It'd rung once, twice, and just as the third ring was about to end, there was a short silence of the call being answered.

"Jae, I really hope you aren't calling to ask me to give you her number again," Jisung's voice was expectant as he said these words, as if he knew for sure that was what he was calling about.

Jaemin wouldn't of minded to smart off to his old friend any other time, but as his eyes dared to look back down to the body of the dead soul, he knew it wasn't time for that. "Jisung, I think you're going to want to get outside, to the alleyway on the left side of the school, behind the gym."

There was another short silence, before Jisung's confused voice broke it, "what? Why, what are you trying to do?"

Sighing, Jaemin only mumbles, "just come, you're going to want to see this."



Chapter twenty eight; adversity

Chenle had to turn away the moment the three boys had walked up to where Jaemin had told them to. Being that he was no doubt the weakest out of the entirety of their gang, it wasn't easy for him to see these sorts of things. Sure, Chenle didn't mind violence, he didn't mind the blood, as long as it wasn't for one of them.

Which is why he couldn't hold in his emotion the second he laid eyes on their beloved Jeno. Turning his back immediately to the scene, his hand goes to cover his mouth as his eyes well with tears. He didn't want the others to see him cry, but at the same time, he couldn't help it, as he silently wept about the loss of his friend.

Renjun is silent, just like the other three. Jaemin could only watch their expressions, feeling pity for the boys even though they literally tried to kill him.

Unlike the other two, Jisung looked angered more than he looked sad. The boy looked as if he was ready to kill an entire country of people, as he bent over to inspect his friend's dead body closer. His brown eyes narrow, and the others furrow their brows, confused as to what he was doing as he'd stuck a hand down the pocket of Jeno's denim jacket.

No one had spoken a word. Nothing needed to be said, the three boys knew well of what happened and why it happened. Jaemin didn't know what he could say to them, he didn't have any idea what was going on.

And the moment that Jisung had unfolded the piece of paper to reveal the words upon it, their suspicions as to why their friend was now dead were only confirmed further.

bite us, we bite back harder
xoxo

(a/n: gossip girl said wus good)

"What sort of sick fuck puts xoxo on a note of someone he just murdered?" Renjun had snapped in exasperation as he read the note over his leader's shoulder.

Chenle couldn't find the words to say due to how emotionally weak he was feeling. He only shook his head sadly, burying his face in his hands as he mumbles incoherent things to himself.

"They really fucking did this," Jisung is saying in a low mumble, his voice dark and no doubt pissed. As he read it over and over, repeating the words on the rancid note in his head, he couldn't help but think back to what Mark said that night.

There's something dark coming, Jisung, you have to be ready to face it.

He never asked what it was he meant by that. Jisung hadn't believed it was important enough, he figured their elder was once again just talking nonsense. After all, in Jisung's opinion that was all Mark ever did. He just endlessly ran his mouth saying things no one understood, and gave pointless lectures.

But maybe it hadn't been so pointless after all.

Running a hand through his hair, Jisung - for once - felt some sort of emotion as he turned away from his friend's body. He didn't look in the eyes of any of the three boys as he only says, "Jae, help them move his body to the trunk, will ya?"

Jaemin blinks a few times as he takes in the words which he had just heard. Renjun and Chenle were already moving to pick up the boy's lifeless form, and he could only stare at their actions, trying to process what was going on. Surely he doesn't think we're suddenly buddies.

"Look, I don't know what sort of business you've got going on, but I was just trying to do the right thing," he clears his throat as he speaks to Jisung, who is now standing only feet away. His arms are crossed over his chest as he stares off into the horizon, most likely pondering what their next move should be after this. "But this doesn't mean I'm suddenly a part of whatever you're all supposed to be."

As Jaemin had finished his statement, an ill silence had filled the atmosphere. The two boys were still waiting for their help with carrying the body, and Jisung had slowly turned from where he had been staring into nothingness.

Slowly but surely, a long, deep sigh left his lips. He meets Jaemin's eyes, and for some reason, there was pity in his brown irises, as if he was speaking to a fool, "Jae," he shakes his head, "you were involved the second you stepped foot into DMHS."

His words had left confusion in the brain of Na Jaemin once again. Before he could even begin to ask what that was supposed to mean, Jisung had turned on his heel to walk to their car. Jaemin felt stressed, no doubt, as he looked back to the two boys.

They'd only shrugged once they caught his look. The two of them looked shaken up still, and Chenle was still crying silent tears.

With the way the two of them looked, he couldn't help but feel like he didn't have a choice. So, with a heavy exhale, Jaemin had walked over to help them move the body of the newly passing gang member.




~




"Hye, it's okay," Haechan soothes, his arms wrapped so tightly around her that he was surprised she could still breathe. It was as if he was afraid to let go, as if she'd disappear in an instant if his grip got even a little weaker, and in a way - he was. "Whoever that was, he's dead, you're hallucinating, it's not real."

His honey like voice was transformed into a calming whisper. Such a sound send shivers through out her entire body, and she found herself meeting his soft brown irises. Hye's mind hadn't been in the right state then, she didn't have control of what was going on inside her.

"Haechannie," she mumbles his name in a small voice, "I'm still scared."

The boy that held the girl so tightly, pursed his lips. He wasn't sure what to say anymore. After all, Haechan knew that the side effects of whatever drug that was. It hadn't been anything they would carry, right? Or had someone like Jisung gotten stronger drugs just for such an occasion? There were many possibilities, and despite his intelligent wit, he didn't know which one was right.

That fact angered him more than anything else. For some reason, Haechan felt the want to protect Hye. He didn't want anything bad to happen to her, not now, not ever.

Such a fact was why he only leaned his forehead against hers, her legs wrapped around his waist and her small body facing his. Her green irises poor into his as he assures her, "you'll be okay, everything will be okay. I won't let anything happen to you."

That was the last thing he had gotten to say to her then. Before you knew it, Hyeyeon had gotten tired from the toll the drug was still taking on her fragile body. In only a moment, the girl had passed out again. It was then that Haechan had set her softly atop his mattress, pulling his duvet over her body.

He rose to his feet then, running a hand through his hair as he pondered on just what exactly was going on. Haechan was the sort of person who despised being clueless. If something was going on, he needed to know exactly what it was. If he didn't, it'd drive him to insanity.

His eyes fall on the sleeping girl once again. Just the sight of her made him feel a way he wasn't sure he could admit, even to himself. It caused him to turn his back to her, groaning to himself as he tried to process anything. What was getting into him? Why did he feel so attached to this girl?

Haechan's thoughts are cut short by the feeling of his phone vibrating angrily in his back pocket. A sigh of annoyance leaves his lips as he immediately knows who it most likely is, probably going to ask of his whereabouts. As he pulls his phone out of his pocket, he had not even the slightest intention of telling him jack shit, because whether Jisung was apparently the 'leader' or not, Haechan wasn't ever going to bow down to him like everyone else.

Seeing the name on his phone screen, even though it was who he suspected, still made him groan. In disgust, he slides his phone across the screen, shoving the device to his ear. Not even a millisecond had passed when he'd snarled, "what the fuck do you want?"

During any other time, Jisung would've been happy to argue with the sarcastic smart ass that Lee Haechan was. He never missed a moment to anger the boy even more, being fully aware of how he wasn't very fond of him because of the previous competition that had arose between the two. And since Jisung had won what Haechan had so rightfully deserved, he'd never forgive him.

Now especially that Haechan knew Hye. Knowing how he had ruined her life, he had always sought that it wasn't right even despite his careless manner. However, he had never known her personally to care enough.

But now that he did, he couldn't believe Jisung had the audacity to do things like that to her.

To Haechan's dismay, Jisung had only let out a shaky breathe on the other line. It sounded as if he had turned into a different person when he cleared his throat, at first sounding shattered before his voice went back to the normal, aggressive state, "I need you to get the fuck down here, sorry to cut off your boning session with whatever random girl you picked up."

He couldn't help but grow annoyed by the comment. Sure, Haechan had had his fair share of girls through out the years. It wasn't like he as provocative or anything, but girls had always thrown themselves at him. So, why would he not take their offers sometimes? It was like saying no to people giving you a free money, who does that?

Even though it was common knowledge he did things like that, he hadn't anymore. Not in a long time, not since he met Hyeyeon.

He was about to speak up, when he heard low mumble's in the background. The voice was immediately recognizable as the drug dealer himself. "Uh, actually, I'm pretty sure I saw Haechan leave with Hyeyeon."

The anger had flew up his throat like a wildfire. Now he knows she's at the house, Haechan couldn't help but groan as he angrily called into the phone, "Renjun, I hope you know when I see your lanky ass I am going to beat the living fuck-," he was cut off by Jisung's menacing chuckles.

"Hear that, Jae? The whore left with my boy Haechan here, and I think we all know where that went."

His brown irises bulge as he takes in Jisung's words that were targeted at - Jaemin? Although he was unsure of why he would be there, he assumed after what had happened when he went to pick her up that Jaemin had ended up showing up first. Haechan couldn't really be mad about it, firstly because for some reason - despite his temper - he couldn't be mad at Hyeyeon. And secondly, because it wasn't like she knew anyway, right?

Assuming the two of them attended together, Haechan still couldn't help but feel a little jealous, and angry. Had he let this happen to her? Shouldn't he have kept a closer eye out and been a little more cautious? He couldn't believe how careless it was all playing out in his head, and it made him less fond of Jaemin despite not knowing him.

He knew what Jisung was making Jaemin think. Even though it wasn't true at all, a part of Haechan wanted him to possibly think it was.

That was, if she hadn't been drugged.

"You're a fucking idiot, Hyeyeon wasn't okay, she needed to get home," Haechan was quick to defend, "someone drugged her drink with something strong. I'd like to hope it wasn't you."

There was a snort on the other line, no doubt coming from Jisung. "Oh, you too? I already went through this with Jae here," Jisung had begun to lowly laugh, before the sound of him presumably patting Jaemin's shoulder was heard, "sounds like you've got some competition, bud."

Through out the entire time, Jaemin hadn't said a word. He was smart enough to know Jisung was trying to purposely start drama, to anger one of them and cause a scene. It was what Jisung loved to do, practically his hobby. It was why he wouldn't let it work, not on him.

He could hear Haechan's words from the phone being as such a high volume. From the way he talked so fondly of Hyeyeon, it seemed as if they were friends. Although he didn't know well of this, he decided that it seemed that she was in good hands. She was safe, and he tried his best to believe that.

But at the end of the day, Haechan was still a gang member - in Jisung's gang.

"Is she okay?" is what Jaemin had finally asked, directing it at the boy that was with her.

There was a short pause, before Haechan had hummed, "she's dandy, still asleep after a couple of hours, and I'm sure her head is gonna hurt when she's awake, but the effects should wear off by then."

"Damn," Renjun is mumbling, his voice still weak and shaken from the previous events, "what the hell was the drug?" He and Chenle had seen the way she had been acting, it was fucking scary. It was unlike anything he had ever seen despite being someone who mixed drugs himself.

"Sounds like it wasn't you guys, then," Haechan had presumed, ignoring Renjun's question.

Jisung sighs as if he should've already concluded that, "obviously."

"Fuck," Haechan curses. A part of him had actually wanted it to be his stupid members. At least then he could call them useless fiends and get it over with, probably even beat them upside the head.

However, knowing that it wasn't them, meant that he didn't know who it was. And that drove him insane.

"Uh, hello?! Can we get back to the real issue here?!" Chenle was rather upset that everyone was just so casually ignoring the fact their friend was dead. He still couldn't seem to process it, and even now, the tears were still coming. All those times he and Jeno had spent together playing games and just telling jokes, they were gone. He understood he'd done bad things, they'd all done bad things. But at the end of the day, they were still people. They still had feelings, and family (aka each other,) and they still felt remorse and emotion even if it was rare.

He didn't deserve it. I wish it was me instead.

At the sight of Chenle in tears again, Renjun had gave him a side hug. The two boys embraced each other, and although it made their usual bad ass masculine look disappear for a moment, they both needed it more than anything.

Haechan heard the commotion through the speaker, and was more lost than anything. "So, what exactly did you call me for?"

The silence that was usually short lived, felt as if it lasted a lifetime. No one had the energy to say it, and the four boys kept exchanging looks, as if telling each other to do it because they didn't have the strength.

Finally, Jisung had let out a deep breathe. He runs a hand through his hair, using his other hand to still hold the phone in front of him, and in that moment, as the wind seemed to ever so slightly blow against their skin, he felt the emotion he had been trying so hard not to feel. They always swore to protect each other, but tonight they'd failed. And even though Jisung was never the best leader, he still tried.

Sure, he got caught up in his own antics sometimes. Maybe he was a little on the selfish side. But he still loved his members like his brothers, they saved him.

And now he had failed with his job as not only a brother, but a leader, to save Jeno in return.

This exact thought it what caused him to finally break as he cleared his throat many more times before he was able to speak, "Jeno's been murdered."


Chapter twenty nine; new alliances

Sunlight beamed through the small cracks in the curtains from the few windows in the room. A boy had entered the room, his aura that of a witty old man, as he stood beside the bed. His brown irises peer down at the sleeping girl, who seemed to still be asleep soundly, as if nothing in the world could bother her.

Slowly but surely, he bends over, reaching his hand out to slightly place it atop her head to check her temperature.

That was when she stirred, it was only a little at first, but after another split second had passed, Hyeyeon had shot up like an animal in the bed. Her green eyes were widened in alert, and she looked as if she was 100% ready to attack whoever might be in the same room as her.

Her eyes rake across the room she most definitely didn't recognize. Hurriedly, she racks her brain for any information of her whereabouts. But she couldn't remember anything. Hye felt astonished, had I drank at the Halloween party? It didn't sound like anything she would do, she never drank.

So why was her memory so iffy? All she remembered was arriving with Jaemin after having had met him at her house.

"Um-," the boy had awkwardly spoke when she still hadn't noticed him standing beside the bed. The second she heard his voice, she turned into some sort of lunatic as she squealed, scurrying out of the bed and onto her feet. Hyeyeon had jumped right in front of him, preparing her fists to punch the living shit out of him.

The sight of her getting into such a position caused him to put his hands up in defense, "Whoa, whoa, calm down," he assures her in a calming tone. Her eyes are narrowed as they peer up at him, and she tries to process just who the fuck this was - and where she was. "You must be Hyeyeon," he'd concluded.

"Where the fuck am I, and who are you?" she's quick to snap, throwing questions at him like a mad man.

The boy couldn't help but chuckle at her defensive, strong attitude, thinking of the way Haechan had talked to him about her when he had left to go to the high school (although he hadn't told him why.) Never had he known much about Jisung's ex girlfriend, or how she acted, but now that he was meeting her, she reminded him a lot of Haechan. No wonder he seemed so attached to her.

"You're at Dream's house, and I'm Mark," he finally tells her, but nothing he was saying was making her any less confused. The look on her face almost caused him to laugh again, but he held it in as he explained further, "this might scare you, but it's Jisung's gang's HQ, if you may. My name is Mark, I'm the old leader."

She was slowly putting the pieces together as to who he was, but the fact she was at Jisung's house made her want to puke. Not to mention how her head was aching, was she sleeping in his bed? She wasn't sure if she wanted to know.

"Okay, so now would you like to inform me why the fuck I am here?"

He couldn't help but laugh out loud that time. It was just so funny to him how alike she was to his best friend. Mark honestly found it hysterical, and she was looking at him like a mental patient as he'd sat there giggling for a second.

"Sorry," he quickly cleared his throat, "Haechan brought you here, don't worry. This is his room, and I'm his best friend, not one of the dogs." Mark knew well of how she felt about Jisung, and his dogs, as Haechan had explained. He felt it was necessary to reassure her he wasn't like that.

At the mention of Haechan, Hyeyeon's nerves had resigned. Looking around again at the room which she stood in, it wasn't exactly what she imagined a gang members bedroom to look like. Either way, it made her feel rather homey, and she sighs as she falls back to sit on the edge of the mattress.

"Where is Haechan?" she asks curiously, raising a brow at the boy whom she had just met. Again, Hye didn't really trust anyone very easily, or at least she tried not to. But since she trusted Haechan, and this was apparently his best friend, that meant he must be trustworthy.

Mark shrugs, shoving his hands in his pockets, "I don't really know, apparently there's some business that needed to be taken care of back at the highschool. It sounded rather serious."

Hyeyeon blinks up at him a few times, wondering what it was now that they'd gotten into. The events of that night at the alleyway on the abandoned side of town replay in her head, and she hurriedly flushes them out. Don't think about it, she assures herself, it had to be done.

She remembers well how her best friend, Sicheng, was also in a gang. If she thinks back to that night, Haechan had been going to deal with another gang, had he not? Conveniently, Sicheng had ran into him around that time.

That thought set a bad feeling in her stomach.

At the thought of Cheng, she remembers she hadn't spoken to him still.

"You look really confused, I'm sure you have a lot of questions," Mark observes, causing her to jump a bit from having been so caught up in her own thoughts. "He'll be back soon, and I'm sure Haechan will tell you everything."

She only offers him a small smile, "uh, thanks, Mark."

"Sure," he shrugs, "by the way, you probably want some headache medicine, huh?"





~







Haechan felt like his body was lifeless as he drove to the highschool. It was so mind blowing for him to believe, and he didn't want to. He didn't want it to be true, that his friend was really no longer living. That he was no longer going to be around them anymore. Even though Haechan wasn't fond of the other members anymore, they were still his only family. They were still the only people he'd had for the longest time, and at one point, they really did act like a family even though they didn't anymore.

And that family, had always included Jeno.

With him gone, it would never feel right. They had lost not only their main source of gun power and weaponry, but their brother. It caused a painful ping to shoot into his heart every few seconds as he turned the BMW into the parking lot, driving to where he saw Jisung and the others parked.

The four boys were all gathered around the closed trunk, where he presumed beloved Jeno was. Trying his hardest not to think about it, Haechan forced any emotion to the back of his mind as he parked the car beside them. Turning off the ignition, he takes the keys out and shoves them in his pocket, climbing out of the vehicle.

It's silence as he walks up to them. Renjun was still patting Chenle's back every so often to calm the boy's nerves. Just knowing how soft Chenle was as a human being, it almost made Haechan frown at the sight of how torn up the boy was. Even Renjun was fighting back his own tears, and the sight of his brothers in such a way angered him.

But what really set Haechan off, was the sight of Jisung looking so casual. It was like nothing in the world was wrong. And although he was most likely doing what Haechan himself did on a daily basis and hiding it, it still pissed him off.

Either way, whether Jisung was feeling any emotion about the situation or not, it was all still his fault. As a leader, he had failed not only Jeno, but all of them. Not even this once, but countless times. Everything Jisung had ever done as a leader was a fail. Never had he cared about anything more than himself, and just that thought was the reason Jeno was dead.

Unable to control his rage, Haechan stepped forward, raising his fist without a second thought and slammed his fist into his jaw. There was the sound of a crack as the skin had collided with bone, and the three boys that had just witnessed the event had gasped in surprise.

Shocked at what just happened, Jisung stumbled back against the trunk of his car. His hands go to hold his hurt jaw, and he shifts his head side to side as if to move it back into place.

Slowly, his brown, dark eyes glare into Haechan's. No doubt, he was pissed by the action the boy had just performed, but for once, instead of injuring him back, he tried to be the bigger person. "What the fuck was that for?!"

Crossing his arms over his chest, Haechan only had to say one word, "Jeno."

Renjun and Chenle had managed to break a chuckle despite what they were feeling. Even they felt like the action was well deserved.

Jisung groans in annoyance, shaking his head as he looks away. For once, he felt like he was in fault, which was why he took Haechan's punch, only sighing as he leaned back against his car.

"It's your fault, don't forget that," he felt the need to remind the so called leader.

"I know!" Jisung had snapped, still holding the side of his jaw where he had been punched. A bruise would definitely be forming there soon. His voice once loud and mighty, Jisung's next words were that of a kitten as he mumbled, "I know it's my fault."

"Good, I hope you understand we shouldn't mess with them now."

There's a long silence, and Haechan took that as the time to divert his eyes to Jaemin. The boy had been awkwardly sitting there, staring at his phone. He looked rather sad, like he was lost in his own head. He wondered then just why he was here, as in the first place it had probably been to ask Jisung about Hye. But why was he sticking around so long?

"Actually," Jisung finally hums, "I think I want to do the exact opposite."

"What?" Chenle and Renjun had seemed to voice in unison. You could tell they were both realizing how big of an idiot their leader was, maybe they'll stop listening to him like slaves now.

Standing up straight from his previous position, Jisung voices, "how about we go right back after them? They want to play dirty, let's play dirty," there's an undeniable smirk plastered on his face, and his eyes move back to Haechan, "Don't you still know where they're located at?"

He didn't want to answer the question honestly. Whatever idiotic idea Jisung was cooking up in his head was probably going to be terrible, and the last thing it'd result in was most likely getting more of them killed.

However, at the same time, a part of him was still intrigued. If he answered yes or no, it wasn't like he was telling him where, which is why he shrugs, "perhaps."

"Exactly," Jisung says as if he's some sort of genius, "we can't let Jeno's death be in vain, this is war."

The others exchange looks, trying to decide if what he was saying was actually intelligent or not. The thing was, you couldn't really trust someone like Jisung to ever say anything not completely ridiculous. But what he was saying now, wasn't exactly far fetched. Sure, Haechan knew that his old gang was smarter than them, but was it really because of skill? Or were they just not thinking hard enough?

He purses his lips, unsure of what to say. "You're going to talk to Mark about this before you start anything stupid."

Jisung only nods, pulling his keys out of his pocket. "I know, which is why we're going to take care of our brother here," he pats the trunk, referring to the fact they couldn't just leave Jeno's poor body in there, "before heading home."

"We're not having that conversation tonight, are we? I think we all need some rest," Renjun says as he has an arm wrapped around Chenle's shoulders. The both of them still didn't look so good.

Jisung shakes his head, "No, tomorrow," he turns to walk to the drivers side of the car, thus dismissing everyone, before he looks to Jaemin, "thanks for the insight and help, Jae, you just might be our new recruit." Jisung had pulled out his phone, opening the message app and going to him and Jaemin's contacts, where he sent him a certain amount of numbers. Winking to the boy as Jaemin's phone had dinged in his pocket, he hums, "consider us even, I'll call you."

And with that, they headed home.

But the second he entered the house and saw all the guys sitting on the couch, the second he realized Jeno wasn't there, and that he never would be again.

It was like reality had suddenly slapped him in the face. He'd practically ran back up to his room, just wanting to be alone to finally release all the emotion he had been holding in for so long.

However, he'd forgotten about the fact Hye was literally in his bedroom. And now it was too late to turn back and pretend like this had never happened, she'd already witnessed his weak side, which was what he never wanted anyone to see.

Just staring down at her small body, he's reminded of what happened to her last night. He's reminded of the fact there is someone else out there, someone else who gave her those drugs without her knowing. There's someone else, who had only single handed-ly targeted her.

With everything, everything that had happened in such a short amount of time, he no longer felt like the strong boy he always tried to be. For the first time in forever, Haechan felt weak.

She was the only one who had ever witnessed him in such a way, but weirdly enough, he didn't mind that, with the way she was standing so close their faces were only inches apart. Her green eyes seem to peer up at him in curiosity and sympathy, and he can tell she feels empathy for the fact he'd lost a brother that night. Her hands are hesitant as they reach towards his face, where she runs her thumb against his jaw, until it was to his forehead, where she pushes his fringe out of his face.

In that moment, Haechan wanted to tell her. He wanted to tell her that he knew who had killed his brother, that her best friend was a murderer. Although he was unaware that she already knew of Sicheng's actions in the gang, he wanted her to know all of it. He wanted her to know the sort of monstrous things they really did.

127 was more dangerous than the Dreamies could ever be. Haechan and Mark had created this gang after leaving them for maybe not a good reason to the public eye, but a good reason to them. They couldn't take the sort of dark things they were being forced to do, the sort of careless acts they had to partake in. All they wanted was to get by, to sell so they had enough money to put food before them. They wanted to live like teenagers, and go to parties and for once - just pretend like they're normal.

All the two boys ever wanted to be just that - young. They wanted to embrace their youth, not kill people.

However, despite these opinions and desires, as he closed his eyes as if to take in the feeling of Hyeyeon's soft finger tips in his hair, he knew it, he knew what was coming.

Haechan knew what had to be done. And although he wasn't a fan of the mission, there was no avoiding it. It was to avenge Jeno.

And for his brother, he would do anything.

If it wasn't Jisung, who else would've done it - and had their hands on such a drug in the first place?

That meant a lot to her.

He's quiet for a long while, trying to put together the words he wishes to say.

He hadn't been sure if he wanted to inform her of this, but it was better now than never. If someone was after Hyeyeon, the only lead he had to know who it was, was asking Hyeyeon herself.

Without a second thought, her feet pad across the carpeted floor of his bedroom, and the fragile girl climbs on the mattress, sitting beside him. Her actions cause Haechan's eyes to look to her, and there's an emotion she hadn't yet seen from him hidden deep within his irises.

"I don't know, Hye."

She had to swallow the lump in her throat. Was someone after her? It was a surreal thought she didn't want to think of, why? Hyeyeon hadn't ever really done anything wrong. She wasn't truly guilty of everything her classmates accused her of. Despite her strong attitude, she was that of a child.

The poor girl wasn't involved in a gang, she didn't take part in any violent acts. And she wasn't even as rude as she came off as.

Why would someone want to do that to her?

"Hey," his honey like voice breaks through her worried thoughts, and when she looks to Haechan, he sees the clear fear in her green eyes. It was a sight he knew all too well, one that brought him back to a dark time, and it was what impaled him to tell her, "I won't let anything happen to you, okay? I promise."



Chapter thirty one; tension

A loud, abrupt yawn leaves Haechan's lips as his feet trot down the steps of the place he called home. His eyes were still half closed, and his body still didn't feel like it was moving at all. As he reaches the bottom of the steps to round his way into the living area, only then did his brain even fully wake up to process what was going on - and remember everything that had happened.

What's usually a lively, bright house of idiotic teenage boys was the complete opposite that Saturday afternoon. The now four boys sat on the many sofas that surrounded the living room of the house, and the room was dead silent. Not even the TV was on, nor was Jisung blasting his rap music through the speakers that hung on the walls.

Under any other circumstances, he would've loved the otherwise pleasant silence. But knowing why they were this way, knowing what they were about to have to even speak about, ruined it all. The quiet instead became deadly to him as he pats across the carpet, meeting the eyes of only three out of the four boys.

Haechan falls onto the double sofa beside Mark, the room being so noiseless you heard the sound of his body hitting the seat with a plop. Even then, as a deep sigh left his lips, and he overlooks to his friends, no one spoke a word.

Renjun had his head leaned back against the top of the couch, staring up at the ceiling in thought. Chenle had his head on the boy's shoulder, his gaze fixated on the floor that he stared at. Every few seconds, you would see tears well in his otherwise shining orbs, that he would then quickly blink away. And his best friend Mark, who he assumed they had already broke the news to due to the way he was also looking rather bitter, had his arms crossed over his chest, bouncing his leg up and down against the floor. His face was that of mixed emotions. Haechan could tell he was upset, how could he not be? Knowing Mark, he was probably blaming it all on himself, because deep down, he still was the leader. But a part of him seemed angry, undeniably angry, at himself, Jisung, and especially their old gang mates.

He looked so angry that in fact, even though Mark was known for being against violence, he looked ready to kill. Whether he wasn't a fan of such acts or not, he'd do anything when it came to protecting and avenging his brothers.

"So," Jisung had cleared his throat, "I - have a plan." His words were shaky and hesitant for once, as if he was thinking very carefully about everything he was saying. It was actually the most thoughtful Haechan had ever seen the sack of shit in his life. He didn't even think Jisung had ever used his brain.

No doubt he must've noticed Mark's anger, and even he managed to be afraid of the elder.

"It better be a damn good one," was what Mark had snapped, his eyes narrowed as he finally looked to the orange haired boy sitting on the opposite side of Renjun and Chenle.

Swallowing the lump in his throat, he nods slowly, "we just have to find where they're located, we can get them when they least expect it."

Everyone had looked up to the sound of these words leaving his lips. They all knew what he meant, he meant violence. However, they weren't exactly sure what type the new found leader was speaking of.

"What?" Renjun says, "you mean kill one of them?"

It was clear from the way the nerves seemed to leave his facial expression that Jisung had quite the idea on his mind. "No, I mean much more than that."

Immediately, everyone in the room looks to Mark. Whether Jisung was now the leader or not, Mark would always still be the higher up in power. Being the founder of the reason they were all even still alive, he always had first say in whether they did something or not - or at least he was supposed to. But God knew Jisung usually didn't like to play by the rules.

Since not playing by the rules had led to Jeno's death, though, he seemed to be rethinking it.

"Interesting," the eldest had finally voiced, "but I'm not sure where you're gonna get info like that."

Jisung's brows furrow as he'd said these words, as this was clearly a dent in his thought process. "Don't you both remember where it was?" he asks as if it should've been obvious.

However, at this, Mark bursts into bitter laughter. Even Haechan couldn't help but giggle at his stupidity, and in return to the two boys snickering in disappointment, Jisung's previously triumphant expression vanished.

"What?" he asks when they still didn't say anything because of the way they kept chuckling.

Shaking his head, a sigh leaves the lips of the boy who had yet to speak until then, "it would've been idiotic for them to stay at the same house after all these years, they've clearly moved locations."

You could tell the way Jisung tried to hide the defeat that still obviously took over his face. And just like that, the five of them were left yet again in a pool of defeat, just this time with a minus one.

Haechan internally groaned as he thought about it. He hated not knowing what to do with everything that was going on, not to mention the fact there was still a sleeping girl in his bedroom.

As if there was some sort of telepathy between the boys, in that moment Renjun had quietly spoke up, "what about Hyeyeon?"

His brown irises immediately widen in surprise at the mention of the girl's name. He had a good feeling as to what he was suggesting, and before he could even open his mouth to abruptly voice his opinion on that suggestion, Jisung had first, "the fuck are you bringing that bitch up for?"

"Go fuck yourself," he'd growled instead, meant towards no one other than her ex boyfriend. Haechan had never gotten along with the idiot, but now that he was friends with Hyeyeon, he only hated him more. It was so difficult for him to even be in the same room with him, and hearing him speak about her in such a way like she ever did anything to him only appalled him more.

Jisung only glared right back at Haechan before looking back to Renjun. He felt a little awkward due to the obvious tension in the room, but still continued anyway, "isn't she still friends with Sicheng? I heard Haechan talking to him back at the South side."

You're fucking kidding me.

It took everything for Haechan not to rise straight to his feet before proceeding to throw the only thing separating him and Renjun directly at his face - which was a table. "Whatever you're tiny fucking brain is suggesting, it's a no."

Renjun frowns from his words, but shakes his head to dismiss what Haechan had said, "Surely she knows, and if she doesn't, we can get her to find out."

A smirk had spread over Jisung's lips, and the boy sitting beside Mark knew that he was already working something up in his brain. The poor girl already had enough on her plate without these baboons adding to it.

"She's not going to help you imbeciles, and I won't let her, either."

Everyone is surprised by his outburst as he'd rose to his feet to glare at all of them. "Why do you care so much? What's the harm, huh?" Jisung had cooed, but it was clear he had a good idea of just what was going on with Haechan.

Clenching his fists, he narrows his eyes directly at the boy before snarling, "why the literal fuck would she want to help you, anyway?"

He only shrugs casually, "because," he hums, "you're going to get her to."

The way he'd said this was so matter of factly, which only added to how funny Haechan found it. "fuck you, I'm not helping you either."

Jisung shakes his head, making a tsk tsk sound with his teeth as he meets the frustrated gaze of the standing being before him, "Sad, not even for Jeno."

That - struck something inside of him.

For once, he didn't know what to say. It was for Jeno, and it wasn't like anything would happen to her.

Running a hand through his hair in stress, he exhales a deep breathe. "We'll see," is all he says, before making his way back up the steps to his bedroom, defeated and conflicted.

Meanwhile, Hyeyeon was sitting on the edge of the bed which she'd only woken up from around an hour ago. She'd actually woke up only shortly after Haechan, and had stepped out into the hall from his room cautiously. It didn't take her long to hear the commotion downstairs, and she realized that it wasn't her business or place to strut down there like she actually lived here.

In fact, she was feeling like she had over stayed her welcome. Truthfully, Hyeyeon didn't know what was going on with her friend anymore. All she was trying to do was help Haechan because she knew he was lost because of his friends murder, and not to mention he was helping her as well. They just had a close friendship, right?

Or was there something more?

Either way, she wasn't mentally prepared to own up to what her heart was saying. There were too many confused feelings in the back of her head, too many thoughts clouding her brain. Someone was after her, and even though Haechan promised he wouldn't let anything happen, could she really believe him? He couldn't always be with her, and the fact she didn't know who would want anything with her terrified her.

Unintentionally, Hyeyeon had gotten herself more involved in the gang life than she'd planned. Perhaps it happened when she dealt with Jisung two years ago, trying to get him to not involve himself. Thanks to him, back then, she'd been involved the entire time.

Now that she was still friends with Sicheng even after their fight, plus Haechan. Maybe there were more people on the look out for her than she knew of.

A sigh had left her lips as she forces her voice to sound bright and cheery like usual, holding the phone to her ear. Her green eyes are peering at the wall as she'd told Sicheng the address to the home which she'd stayed in for too long. She no longer felt like being cooped up in Haechan's room, (plus he probably was tired of her,) and the last thing she wanted was to see any of the dogs, or especially the dog himself.

"Ah, alright, I'm on my way now, Hye," Sicheng's voice had broke through her everlasting thoughts, him sounding happier than usual. Unsure as to why, she assumed it was just because she'd given in and finally ended their fight, so she shook it off.

"Okay," she mumbles, "thanks, Chengie."

Little was she aware of the boy that had been standing on the other side of the closed bedroom door. Haechan had heard the last few words of her conversation, meaning her heard her just give a 127 member their address.

It took all of him not to slam his head right into the wall beside him. Instead, he closes his eyes for a moment and deeply exhales to calm his screaming nerves. The small girl purses her lips for a moment, staring up at him in thought. "Uh, no worries," she finally hums, "my best friend offered to come get me."

Even though he already knew, he only nods, "ah, is he?"

"Yup," she nonchalantly mumbles, and the room fell silent again. Her eyes had diverted back to her phone to reply to another text, and Haechan took that as the time to silently mouth the words god fucking dammit.

This was bad, worse than he wanted it to get. He didn't want to cause anymore stress in her life with asking her to tell him the address of wherever Win was taking her. Despite the fact Hyeyeon had used his real name in the call, he wasn't an idiot and knew well of who he was.

But perhaps he could get it in another way.

He hadn't wanted to do anything like this, and in no way was he using her for information, but it had to be done before they struck first. And he couldn't let that happen, because then when someone got hurt, it'd be his fault.

Haechan couldn't live with anymore guilt, especially not that kind.

There was still a small chance she would remember, and he knew well of how reckless they were. It didn't matter how close you were with someone, if you were friends with the enemy, you didn't get by for free.

Just the thought sends more anxiety up his spine than he could handle. It causes his entire body to shake as he enters the kitchen, having had clenched his fists without knowing.

The five boys were still sitting at the kitchen table as they had been for a while, talking about the plan Jisung had been coming up with. It'd grown silence at the sight of him angrily walking towards them, and in a swift motion Haechan threw the now crumpled piece of paper onto the table before all of them.

Haechan couldn't help but roll his eyes, "No, idiot, I followed her and got it myself. No getting her involved required."

If he wasn't so cold hearted, Jisung would find how desperately Haechan was trying to protect her cute, even. But it only appalled him as he wrinkled his nose in disgust, shaking his head, "she's already fucking involved, she's friends with Sicheng, is she not?"

"That doesn't mean anything."

"Is there not someone after her, as well?"

Closing his eyes to calm his frustration, Haechan clenches his fists at his sides, "we don't fucking know that."

Jisung could tell he was getting angered, and it caused him to smirk. Shrugging it off, he looks back down at the sticky note he held, "sounds to me like she's too close with the enemy - and - is in need of protection."

"She isn't involved with them," he snaps, growing annoyed with all the pointless assumptions Jisung kept making.

"If you say so."

No one says a word, and Mark had sighed at the sight of how upset he was making his best friend. "Leave it alone, Jisung," he commands in disappointment, reaching out to grab the paper from his hands, "focus on what matters, we have the address," looking to Haechan, he offers a reassuring smile, "good job, Haechan."

The boy didn't say anything, he only nods, before turning on his heel and leaving the room. As he did so, he pulls out his phone. More than anything, he wanted to text her, but like an idiot - he still didn't have her number.

Then again, he could ask Jisung, who most likely still had it. But he didn't want to ask that piece of shit for anything. Knowing him, he'd ask for some sort of idiotic favor in return, and he'd be damned if he was going to do anything for him.

A sigh leaves his lips, and he falls onto one of the sofas in the living room whilst logging onto the Instagram app. After all, it was his only source of communication with her. That wouldn't be so bad, if she knew it was him.

Why did he start texting her as this other identity? He wasn't really sure. Using his real name, being this other person, was just him being himself. It felt to him like the real fake identity was Haechan. When he talked to her as Donghyuck, he felt like he could be himself.

As idiotic as it sounded, it was true. He meant everything he had ever told her, including all those compliments and lame flirting attempts. Even how he said the two of them would look great together.

Perhaps it was time for Haechan to be true to himself.

A deep breathe leaves his lips as he goes to the plus sign button, tapping it. Selecting the option to take a photo, he examines himself in the phone camera for a second. There were visible bags under his eyes, and his hair was messier than usual, but despite all of that, he could care less. With a sigh, he snaps the photo, before going on to post it, only putting some emojis under the caption because he wasn't sure of what else to put.

It wasn't long until he'd gotten likes. This was normal for him, as all the girls at DMHS seemed to be obsessed with him, they always had. It was casual, as he watched them comment the weird things like omo, you're so cute, Haechannie~! It was an endless cycle as he'd refresh the notifications tab every few seconds, chuckling to himself at the things they would say.

Only then did he go to the follow requests, scrolling down through them until his brown eyes found a particular one. He wasn't so sure why he felt so unusually nervous as he clicks the green checkmark but her name.

leehyuck has accepted your follow request.

What did that mean when Haechan is the one saying that in the first place?!

Donghyuck, the name repeats in her head, she supposed it was his real name. Today, after all, she'd learned it was common for people to have gang names or more of nicknames. Haechan seemed to be his, the only difference was, literally everyone called him that. She had only heard girls whisper the name Donghyuck, but no one ever directly spoke such a name.

Why is that? she couldn't help but wonder. There were too many questions rolling around her brain as she stares down at his soft face. As expectant of fall to winter weather, it was pouring rain that Sunday. The clock was striking around 7:30 when Haechan had left the house, not caring about the fact the sky was in angry tears. It was the last thing on his mind as he ran through the rain, his car keys tightly clenched in his right hand.

His phone had been in his back pocket, and he hadn't thought Hyeyeon would've texted. If anything, he felt like she might even be a little mad, and especially confused. Why would she not be? Haechan knew he didn't make any sense, that his actions never made any sense. Why would she understand what his motive had been for flirting with her as someone else? Because even he didn't understand it.

That was - until now.

A deep breathe escaped his lips as he unlocked the car, hurriedly climbing inside. Only through out this time had he not noticed the fact his phone fell out of his pocket, onto the wet driveway beneath him.

He hadn't informed anyone of the fact he was leaving, he just didn't care to. The guys hadn't noticed either, they were too busy planning how to get back at 127 and Jeno's funeral, that would be on Monday.

Unsure of what had struck this desire inside of him, he knew it was too late to turn back now. He was just worried, afraid of the thought something could happen to her. Haechan realized that the only thing that could be possible was someone was after her, it was the only thing that made sense. With all the gangs that were in the area, it could be anyone. He didn't know what sort of background or family life she had, but there could be many possibilities as to why someone wasn't a fan of her.

Whether it was connected to him, or Sicheng, or something else, he didn't know. But he did know that any moment he wasn't with her, she wasn't safe.

There was even a possibility it could be 127 themselves. For all he knew they were aware of her close involvement with him, and upset about it. If they hurt her, he wouldn't be able to live with himself.

This is what motivates him to forget about anything else in his life. Haechan couldn't lose anyone else, and he had already dove too deep for this girl to back out now.

With one last glance at himself in the rear view mirror, he slams the pedal on his BMW, and heads towards enemy territory.

Hyeyeon swore her life was a movie recently.

Not having expected anyone to be there.

His words repeat in her head: protection. She definitely needed some of that right now. Where was Haechan when you needed him?

And out of complete fear, she only knew to obey. The rope burnt her wrists as it was tied around them, further preventing her from ever getting away. It was as if her entire life had come crashing down at this moment, as she could feel herself being drug away, down the steps of the porch of the gang house. The rain that was unknowingly pouring from the sky hits her skin, creating more goosebumps than she already had, and she wished that anything could save her then.

Why was it happening? she didn't know the answer. Perhaps it was because of her involvement with Sicheng and Haechan, but why her? Was it because she was the most vulnerable target?

Hyeyeon believed she'd gotten herself involved in something too dark, something darker than the unfortunate ways of high school, something she couldn't and would never be prepared for.

That's what she thought, but little did she know, she'd been involved in it all along.
